# <a name="microsoft-graph-permissions-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-104">Referência de permissões do Microsoft Graph</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-104">Microsoft Graph permissions reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-105">Para que o aplicativo acesse os dados no Microsoft Graph, o usuário ou administrador deve conceder a ele as permissões corretas por meio de um processo de consentimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-105">For your app to access data in Microsoft Graph, the user or administrator must grant it the correct permissions via a consent process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-106">Este tópico lista as permissões associadas a cada grande conjunto de APIs do Microsoft Graph.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-106">This topic lists the permissions associated with each major set of Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-107">Ele também fornece orientações sobre como usar as permissões.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-107">It also provides guidance about how to use the permissions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-108">Para saber mais sobre como funcionam as permissões, [Confira noções básicas de autenticação e autorização](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions) e assista ao vídeo a seguir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-108">To learn more about how permissions work, see [Authentication and authorization basics](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions), and watch the following video.</span></span>

> [!VIDEO https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/yXYzgWWVdSM]

## <a name="microsoft-graph-permission-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-109">Nomes de permissões do Microsoft Graph</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-109">Microsoft Graph permission names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p103">Os nomes de permissões do Microsoft Graph seguem um padrão simples: _resource.operation.constraint_. Por exemplo, _User.Read_ concede permissão para ler o perfil do usuário conectado, _User.ReadWrite_ concede permissão para ler e modificar o perfil do usuário conectado e _Mail.Send_ concede permissão para enviar emails em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p103">Microsoft Graph permission names follow a simple pattern: _resource.operation.constraint_. For example, _User.Read_ grants permission to read the profile of the signed-in user, _User.ReadWrite_ grants permission to read and modify the profile of the signed-in user, and _Mail.Send_ grants permission to send mail on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p104">O elemento _constraint_ do nome determina a extensão potencial do acesso que o aplicativo terá dentro do diretório. No momento, o Microsoft Graph é compatível com as seguintes restrições:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p104">The _constraint_ element of the name determines the potential extent of access your app will have within the directory. Currently Microsoft Graph supports the following constraints:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p105">**Todos** concede permissão para o aplicativo realizar as operações em todos os recursos do tipo especificado em um diretório. Por exemplo, _User.Read.All_ potencialmente concede privilégios ao aplicativo para ler os perfis de todos os usuários em um diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p105">**All** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on all of the resources of the specified type in a directory. For example, _User.Read.All_ potentially grants the app privileges to read the profiles of all of the users in a directory.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p106">**Compartilhado** concede permissão para o aplicativo realizar as operações em recursos que outros usuários compartilharam com o usuário conectado. Essa restrição é usada principalmente com recursos como emails, calendários e contatos do Outlook. Por exemplo, _Mail.Read.Shared_ concede privilégios para ler email na caixa de correio do usuário conectado e emails em caixas de correio que outros usuários na organização compartilharam com o usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p106">**Shared** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on resources that other users have shared with the signed-in user. This constraint is mainly used with Outlook resources like mail, calendars, and contacts. For example, _Mail.Read.Shared_, grants privileges to read mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user as well as mail in mailboxes that other users in the organization have shared with the signed-in user.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p107">**AppFolder** concede permissão para o aplicativo ler e gravar arquivos em uma pasta dedicada no OneDrive. Essa restrição é exposta somente em [Permissões de arquivos](#files-permissions) e só é válida para contas da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p107">**AppFolder** grants permission for the app to read and write files in a dedicated folder in OneDrive. This constraint is only exposed on [Files permissions](#files-permissions) and is only valid for Microsoft accounts.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p108">Se **sem restrição** estiver especificado, o aplicativo estará limitado a executar as operações nos recursos pertencentes ao usuário conectado. Por exemplo, _User.Read_ concede privilégios para ler o perfil apenas do usuário conectado e _Mail.Read_ concede permissão para ler apenas os emails na caixa de correio do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p108">If **no constraint** is specified the app is limited to performing the operations on the resources owned by the signed-in user. For example, _User.Read_ grants privileges to read the profile of the signed-in user only, and _Mail.Read_ grants permission to read only mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-123">**Observação**: Em cenários delegados, as permissões efetivas concedidas ao aplicativo podem ser limitadas pelos privilégios do usuário conectado na organização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-123">**Note**: In delegated scenarios, the effective permissions granted to your app may be constrained by the privileges of the signed-in user in the organization.</span></span>

## <a name="microsoft-accounts-and-work-or-school-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-124">Contas da Microsoft e contas corporativas e de estudante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-124">Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-125">Nem todas as permissões são válidas tanto para contas da Microsoft como para contas corporativas e de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-125">Not all permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-126">Você pode escolher **Conta de suporte da Microsoft** para cada grupo de permissão para determinar se uma permissão específica é válida para contas da Microsoft, contas corporativas ou de estudante ou ambas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-126">You can check the **Microsoft Account Supported** column for each permission group to determine whether a specific permission is valid for Microsoft accounts, work or school accounts, or both.</span></span>

## <a name="permissions-availability-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-127">Status de disponibilidade de permissões</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-127">Permissions availability status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-128">As permissões do Microsoft Graph no [portal do Azure](https://portal.azure.com/) geralmente estão disponíveis e no status DG para todos os aplicativos usarem, exceto alguns conjuntos que estão no status de visualização ou visualização privada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-128">Microsoft Graph permissions in the [Azure portal](https://portal.azure.com/) are generally available and in GA status for all apps to use, except for a few sets that are in preview or private preview status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-129">As permissões na visualização estão disponíveis para o público; elas podem mudar e podem não ser promovidas ao status DG.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-129">Permissions in preview are available to the public; they may change and may not be promoted to GA status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-130">As permissões no status de visualização privada não estão disponíveis e talvez nunca sejam disponibilizadas ao público.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-130">Permissions in private preview status are not and may never become available to the public.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-131">Não use as permissões no status de visualização ou visualização privada em aplicativos de produção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-131">Do not use permissions in preview or private preview status in production apps.</span></span>

## <a name="user-and-group-search-limitations-for-guest-users-in-organizations"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-132">Limitações de pesquisa de usuário e grupo para usuários convidados em organizações</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-132">User and group search limitations for guest users in organizations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-133">Os recursos de pesquisa de usuário e grupo permitem que o aplicativo pesquise usuários ou grupos em um diretório da organização executando consultas no conjunto de recursos `/users` ou `/groups` (por exemplo, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-133">User and group search capabilities allow the app to search for any user or group in an organization's directory by performing queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-134">Os administradores e os usuários têm esse recurso. No entanto, os usuários convidados não.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-134">Both administrators and users have this capability; however, guest users do not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-135">Se o usuário conectado for um usuário convidado, dependendo das permissões que recebeu um aplicativo, ele pode ler o perfil de um usuário específico ou grupo (por exemplo, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`). No entanto, o usuário não pode executar consultas no conjunto de recursos `/users` ou `/groups` que, potencialmente, retornam mais de um recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-135">If the signed-in user is a guest user, depending on the permissions an app has been granted, it can read the profile of a specific user or group (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`); however, it cannot perform queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set that potentially return more than a single resource.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-136">Com as permissões apropriadas, o aplicativo pode ler os perfis de usuários ou grupos que ele obtém seguindo os links nas propriedades de navegação. Por exemplo, `/users/{id}/directReports` ou `/groups/{id}/members`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-136">With the appropriate permissions, the app can read the profiles of users or groups that it obtains by following links in navigation properties; for example, `/users/{id}/directReports` or `/groups/{id}/members`.</span></span>

## <a name="limited-information-returned-for-inaccessible-member-objects"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-137">Informações limitadas retornadas para objetos membro inacessíveis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-137">Limited information returned for inaccessible member objects</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-138">Objetos de contêiner, como grupos, oferecem suporte a membros de vários tipos; por exemplo, usuários e dispositivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-138">Container objects such as groups support members of various types, for example users and devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-139">Quando um aplicativo consulta a associação de um objeto contêiner e não tem permissão para ler um determinado tipo, os membros desse tipo são retornados, mas com informações limitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-139">When an application queries the membership of a container object and does not have permission to read a certain type, members of that type are returned but with limited information.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-140">O aplicativo recebe umas 200 respostas e uma coleção de objetos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-140">The application receives a 200 response and a collection of objects.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-141">Informações completas são retornadas para os tipos de objetos que o aplicativo tem permissões para ler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-141">Complete information is returned for the object types that the application has permissions to read.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-142">Para os tipos de objetos que o aplicativo não tem permissão para ler, apenas o tipo e a ID do objeto são retornados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-142">For the object types which the application does not have permission to read, only the the object type and ID are returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-143">Isso é aplicado a todos as relações que são do tipo [directoryObject](/graph/api/resources/directoryobject) (não apenas aos links de membro).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-143">This is applied to all relationships that are of [directoryObject](/graph/api/resources/directoryobject) type (not just member links).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-144">Os exemplos incluem `/groups/{id}/members`, `/users/{id}/memberOf` ou `me/ownedObjects`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-144">Examples include `/groups/{id}/members`, `/users/{id}/memberOf` or `me/ownedObjects`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-145">Por exemplo, digamos que um aplicativo tenha as permissões de [User.Read.All](#user-permissions) e [Group.Read.All](#group-permissions) do Microsoft Graph.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-145">For example, let's say an application has [User.Read.All](#user-permissions) and [Group.Read.All](#group-permissions) permissions for Microsoft Graph.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-146">Um grupo foi criado e esse grupo contém um usuário, um grupo e um dispositivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-146">A group has been created and that group contains a user, a group, and a device.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-147">O aplicativo chama aos [membros do grupo de listas](/graph/api/group-list-members).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-147">The application calls [list group members](/graph/api/group-list-members).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-148">O aplicativo tem acesso aos objetos de usuário e grupo no grupo, mas não ao objeto do dispositivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-148">The application has access to the user and group objects in the group, but not the device object.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-149">Na resposta, todas as propriedades selecionadas dos objetos de usuário e grupo são retornadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-149">In the response, all the selected properties of the user and group objects are returned.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-150">No entanto, para o objeto de dispositivo, apenas as informações limitadas são retornadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-150">For the device object, however, only limited information is returned.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-151">O tipo de dados e a ID do objeto são retornados para o dispositivo, mas todas as outras propriedades têm um valor *nulo*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-151">The data type and object ID are returned for the device, but all other properties have a value of *null*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-152">Os aplicativos sem permissão não poderão usar a ID para obter o objeto real.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-152">Apps without permission will not be able to use the ID to get the actual object.</span></span>

```http
GET https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/groups/{id}/members?$select=id,displayName,description,createdDateTime,deletedDateTime,homepage,loginUrl HTTP/1.1
```

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-153">Segue a resposta de JSON:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-153">The following is the JSON response:</span></span>

```json
{
"@odata.context":"https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/$metadata#directoryObjects(id,displayName,description,createdDateTime,deletedDateTime,homepage,loginUrl)",
    "value":[
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.user",
            "id":"69d035a3-29c9-469f-809d-d21a4ae69e65",
            "displayName":"Jane Dane",
            "createdDateTime":"2019-09-18T09:06:51Z",
            "deletedDateTime":null
        },
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.group",
            "id":"c43a7cc9-2d95-44b6-bf6a-6392e41949b4",
            "displayName":"Group 1",
            "description":null,
            "createdDateTime":"2019-10-24T01:34:35Z",
            "deletedDateTime":null
        },
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.device",
            "id": "d282309e-f91d-43b6-badb-9e68aa4b4fc8",
            "accountEnabled":null,
            "deviceId":null,
            "displayName":null,
            "operatingSystem":null,
            "operatingSystemVersion":null
        }
    ]
}
```

## <a name="access-reviews-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-154">Permissões de revisões de acesso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-154">Access reviews permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-155">Permissões delegadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-155">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-156">Permissão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-156">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-157">Exibir Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-157">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-158">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-158">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-159">Consentimento Obrigatório do Administrador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-159">Admin Consent Required</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-160">Suporte da conta da Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-160">Microsoft Account supported</span></span> |
|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|:--------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-161">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-161">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-162">Ler todas as revisões de acesso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-162">Read all access reviews</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-163">Permite que o aplicativo leia as revisões de acesso em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-163">Allows the app to read access reviews on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-164">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-164">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-165">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-165">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-166">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-166">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-167">Gerenciar todas as revisões de acesso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-167">Manage all access reviews</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-168">Permite que o aplicativo leia e grave revisões de acesso em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-168">Allows the app to read and write access reviews on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-169">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-169">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-170">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-170">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-171">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-171">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-172">Gerenciar revisões de acesso para participações em grupo e aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-172">Manage access reviews for group and app memberships</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-173">Permite que o aplicativo leia e grave revisões de acesso de grupos e aplicativos em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-173">Allows the app to read and write access reviews of groups and apps on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-174">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-174">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-175">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-175">No</span></span> |


#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-176">Permissões de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-176">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-177">Permissão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-177">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-178">Exibir Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-178">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-179">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-179">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-180">Consentimento Obrigatório do Administrador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-180">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-181">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-181">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-182">Ler todas as revisões de acesso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-182">Read all access reviews</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-183">Permite que o aplicativo leia revisões de acesso sem um usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-183">Allows the app to read access reviews without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-184">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-184">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-189">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-189">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-190">_AccessReview.Read.All_, _AccessReview.ReadWrite. All_ e _AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership _ são válidos apenas para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-190">_AccessReview.Read.All_, _AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_ and _AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-191">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para ler as revisões de acesso de um grupo ou aplicativo, o usuário conectado deve ser membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global, Administrador de Segurança, Leitor de Segurança ou Administrador de Usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-191">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-192">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para gravar revisões de acesso de um grupo ou aplicativo, o usuário conectado deve ser membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global ou Administrador de Usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-192">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-193">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para ler revisões de acesso de uma função do Azure AD, o usuário conectado deve ser um membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global, Administrador de Segurança, Leitor de Segurança ou Administrador de Função Privilegiada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-193">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-194">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para gravar revisões de acesso de uma função do Azure AD, o usuário conectado deve ser membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global ou Administrador de Função Privilegiada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-194">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-195">Para obter mais informações sobre funções de administrador, confira [Atribuindo funções de administrador no Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-195">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-230">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-230">Example usage</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-231">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Ler unidades administrativas (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-231">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Read administrative units (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-232">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Ler lista de membros de uma unidade administrativa (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-232">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Read members list of an administrative unit (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-233">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Criar uma unidade administrativa (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-233">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Create an administrative unit (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-234">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Atualizar uma unidade administrativa (`PATCH /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-234">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Update an administrative unit (`PATCH /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-235">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Adicionar membros a uma unidade administrativa (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-235">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Add members to an administrative unit  (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-236">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-236">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-318">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-318">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-319">A permissão _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ admite as mesmas operações que _Application.ReadWrite.All_, exceto que a anterior só permite essas operações em aplicativos e entidades de serviço que pertencem ao aplicativo de chamada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-319">The _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission allows the same operations as _Application.ReadWrite.All_ except that the former allows these operations only on applications and service principals that the calling app is an owner of.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-320">O proprietário é indicado pela propriedade de navegação `owners` no recurso do [aplicativo](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) ou da [entidade de serviço](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-320">Ownership is indicated by the `owners` navigation property on the target [application](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) or [service principal](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) resource.</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-321">OBSERVAÇÃO: o uso da permissão _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ para chamar `GET /applications` para listar aplicativos falhará com um erro 403.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-321">NOTE: Using the _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission to call `GET /applications` to list applications will fail with a 403.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-322">Use `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` para listar os aplicativos que pertencem ao aplicativo da chamada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-322">Instead use `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` to list the applications owned by the calling application.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-323">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-323">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-324">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-324">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-325">_Application.Read.All_: listar todos os aplicativos (`GET /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-325">_Application.Read.All_: List all applications (`GET /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-326">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: atualizar uma entidade de serviço (`PATCH /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-326">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: Update a service principal (`PATCH /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-327">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-327">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-328">_Application.Read.All_: listar todos os aplicativos (`GET /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-328">_Application.Read.All_: List all applications (`GET /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-329">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: excluir uma entidade de serviço (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-329">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: Delete a service principal (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-330">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: criar um aplicativo (`POST /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-330">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Create an application (`POST /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-331">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Listar todos os aplicativos pertencentes ao aplicativo da chamada (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-331">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: List all applications owned by the calling application (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-332">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: adicionar outro proprietário a um aplicativo próprio (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-332">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Add another owner to an owned application (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`).</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-333">OBSERVAÇÃO: isso pode exigir permissões adicionais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-333">NOTE: This may require additional permissions.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-418">Os Administradores **Importantes** podem configurar a [política de acesso ao aplicativo](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) para limitar o acesso do aplicativo às caixas de correio _específicas_ e não a todas as caixas de correio na organização, mesmo que as permissões de aplicativo do Calendars.Read ou Calendars.ReadWrite sejam concedidas ao aplicativo. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-418">**Important** Administrators can configure [application access policy](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) to limit app access to _specific_ mailboxes and not to all the mailboxes in the organization, even if the app has been granted the application permissions of Calendars.Read or Calendars.ReadWrite.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-419">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-419">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-420">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-420">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-421">_Calendars.Read_: Obter eventos do calendário do usuário entre 23 de abril de 2017 e 29 de abril de 2017 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-421">_Calendars.Read_: Get events on the user's calendar between April 23, 2017 and April 29, 2017 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-422">_Calendars.Read.Shared_: Encontrar horários de reuniões onde todos os participantes estejam disponíveis (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-422">_Calendars.Read.Shared_: Find meeting times where all attendees are available (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-423">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Adicionar um evento ao calendário do usuário (`POST /me/events`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-423">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's calendar (`POST /me/events`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-424">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-424">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-425">_Calendars.Read_: Localizar eventos do calendário de uma sala de conferências organizado por pedro@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-425">_Calendars.Read_: Find events in a conference room's calendar organized by bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-426">_Calendars.Read_: Listar todos os eventos do mês de maio do calendário de um usuário (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-426">_Calendars.Read_: List all events on a user's calendar for the month of May (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-427">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Adicionar um evento de folga aprovada (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`) ao calendário de um usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-427">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to a user's calendar for approved time off  (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-428">_Calendars.Send_: Enviar uma mensagem (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendCalendars`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-428">_Calendars.Send_: Send a message (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendCalendars`).</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="453f9-429">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-429">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-539">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-539">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-540">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-540">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-541">_Calls.Initiate.All_: fazer uma chamada de ponto a ponto do aplicativo para um usuário na organização (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-541">_Calls.Initiate.All_: Make a peer-to-peer call from the application to a user in the organization (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-542">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_: Faça uma chamada em grupo do aplicativo para um grupo de usuários na organização (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-542">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_: Make a group call from the application to a group of users in the organization (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-543">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_: ingressar em uma chamada de grupo ou em uma reunião online do aplicativo (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-543">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-544">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_: Ingresse em uma chamada de grupo ou em uma reunião online do aplicativo, mas o aplicativo só tem privilégios de convidado na reunião (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-544">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application, but the application only has guest privileges in the meeting (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-545">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_: criar ou ingressar em uma chamada e o aplicativo é o acesso direto aos fluxos de participantes de mídia na chamada (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-545">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_: Create or join a call and the app gets direct access to participant media streams in the call (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-546">**Observação:** para obter exemplos solicitação, confira [Criar chamada](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-546">**Note:** For request examples, see [Create call](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-547">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-547">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-743">Os Administradores **Importantes** podem configurar a [política de acesso ao aplicativo](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) para limitar o acesso do aplicativo às caixas de correio _específicas_ e não a todas as caixas de correio na organização, mesmo que as permissões de aplicativo do Contacts.Read or Contacts.ReadWrite sejam concedidas ao aplicativo. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-743">**Important** Administrators can configure [application access policy](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) to limit app access to _specific_ mailboxes and not all the mailboxes in the organization, even if the app has been granted the application permissions of Contacts.Read or Contacts.ReadWrite.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-744">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-744">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-745">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-745">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-746">_Contacts.Read_: Ler um contato a partir de uma das pastas de contatos de nível superior do usuário conectado (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-746">_Contacts.Read_: Read a contact from one of the top-level contact folders of the signed-in user (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-747">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Atualizar a foto de contato de um dos contatos do usuário conectado (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-747">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the contact photo of one of the signed-in user's contacts (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-748">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Adicionar contatos à pasta raiz do usuário conectado (`POST /me/contacts`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-748">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of the signed-in user (`POST /me/contacts`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-749">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-749">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-750">_Contacts.Read_: Ler contatos a parir de uma das pastas de contatos de nível superior de qualquer usuário da organização (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-750">_Contacts.Read_: Read contacts from one of the top-level contact folders of any user in the organization (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-751">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Atualizar a foto de qualquer contato de qualquer usuário em uma organização (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-751">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the photo for any contact of any user in an organization (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-752">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Adicionar contatos à pasta raiz de qualquer usuário da organização (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-752">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of any user in the organization (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-753">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-753">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-833">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-833">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-834">As permissões de diretório fornecem o nível mais alto de privilégio para acessar recursos de diretório, como [Usuário](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0), [Grupo](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) e [Dispositivo](/graph/api/resources/device?view=graph-rest-1.0) em uma organização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-834">Directory permissions provide the highest level of privilege for accessing directory resources such as [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0), [Group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0), and [Device](/graph/api/resources/device?view=graph-rest-1.0) in an organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-835">Elas também controlam exclusivamente o acesso a outros recursos de diretório como: [contatos organizacionais](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta), [APIs de extensão de esquema](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta), [APIs de PIM (Privileged Identity Management)](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta) e muitos dos recursos e APIs listados no nó **Azure Active Directory** na documentação de referência da API beta e v1.0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-835">They also exclusively control access to other directory resources like: [organizational contacts](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta), [schema extension APIs](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta), [Privileged Identity Management (PIM) APIs](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta), as well as many of the resources and APIs listed under the **Azure Active Directory** node in the v1.0 and beta API reference documentation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-836">Isso inclui unidades administrativas, funções de diretório, configurações de diretório, política e muito mais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-836">These include administrative units, directory roles, directory settings, policy, and many more.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-837">A permissão _Directory.ReadWrite.All_ concede os seguintes privilégios:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-837">The _Directory.ReadWrite.All_ permission grants the following privileges:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-838">Leitura completa de todos os recursos de diretório (propriedades declaradas e propriedades de navegação)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-838">Full read of all directory resources (both declared properties and navigation properties)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-839">Criar e atualizar usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-839">Create and update users</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-840">Desabilitar e habilitar usuários (mas não o administrador da empresa)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-840">Disable and enable users (but not company administrator)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-841">Definir a id de segurança alternativa do usuário (mas não administradores)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-841">Set user alternative security id (but not administrators)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-842">Criar e atualizar grupos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-842">Create and update groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-843">Gerenciar associações do grupo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-843">Manage group memberships</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-844">Atualizar o proprietário do grupo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-844">Update group owner</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-845">Gerenciar as atribuições de licença</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-845">Manage license assignments</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-846">Definir as extensões de esquema em aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-846">Define schema extensions on applications</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-847">**Observação**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-847">**Note**:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="453f9-848">Nenhum direito de redefinir senhas de usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-848">No rights to reset user passwords.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="453f9-849">A atualização das propriedades **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone** ou **otherMails** de outro usuário é permitida somente para usuários que não sejam administradores ou que tenham uma das seguintes funções atribuídas: Leitor de Diretório, Emissor de Convites Independente, Leitor do Centro de Mensagens e Leitor de Relatórios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-849">Updating another user's **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone**, or **otherMails** property is only allowed on users who are non-administrators or assigned one of the following roles: Directory Readers, Guest Inviter, Message Center Reader and Reports Reader.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-850">Para obter mais detalhes, confira Administrador de suporte técnico (senha) nas [funções disponíveis do Azure AD](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-850">For more details, see Helpdesk (Password) Administrator in [Azure AD available roles](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-851">Esse é o caso de aplicativos que receberam as permissões User.ReadWrite.All ou Directory.ReadWrite.All delegadas ou de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-851">This is the case for apps granted either the User.ReadWrite.All or Directory.ReadWrite.All delegated or application permissions.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="453f9-852">Nenhum direito de excluir recursos (incluindo usuários ou grupos).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-852">No rights to delete resources (including users or groups).</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="453f9-853">Exclui especificamente a criação ou a atualização de recursos que não estão listados acima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-853">Specifically excludes create or update for resources not listed above.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-854">Isso inclui: application, oAauth2Permissiongrant, appRoleAssignment, device, servicePrincipal, organization, domains e assim por diante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-854">This includes: application, oAauth2Permissiongrant, appRoleAssignment, device, servicePrincipal, organization, domains, and so on.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-855">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-855">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-856">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-856">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-857">_Directory.Read.All_: Listar todas as unidades administrativas em uma organização (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-857">_Directory.Read.All_: List all administrative units in an organization (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-858">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Adicionar membros a uma função de diretório (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-858">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add members to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-859">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-859">Application</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-860">_Directory.Read.All_: Listar todas as associações de um usuário, incluindo funções de diretório e unidades administrativas (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-860">_Directory.Read.All_: List all memberships of a user, including directory roles and administrative units (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-861">_Directory.Read.All_: Listar todos os membros do grupo, incluindo as entidades de serviço (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-861">_Directory.Read.All_: List all group members, including service principals (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-862">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Adicionar um proprietário a um grupo (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-862">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add an owner to a group (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="453f9-863">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-863">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-966">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-966">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-967">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-967">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-968">_EduAssignments.Read_: extrair as informações de atribuição do aluno conectado (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-968">_EduAssignments.Read_: Get the signed-in student's assignment information (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-969">_EduAssignments.ReadWriteBasic_: enviar a tarefa do aluno conectado (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}submit`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-969">_EduAssignments.ReadWriteBasic_: Submit signed-in student assignment (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}submit`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-970">_EduRoster.ReadBasic_: aulas de que um usuário conectado participa como aluno ou professor (`GET /education/classes/{id}/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-970">_EduRoster.ReadBasic_: Classes a signed-in user attends or teaches (`GET /education/classes/{id}/members`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-971">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-971">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1045">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1045">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1046">**Observe** que nas contas pessoais,Files.Read e Files.ReadWrite também concedem acesso a arquivos compartilhados com o usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1046">**Note**: For personal accounts, Files.Read and Files.ReadWrite also grant access to files shared with the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p144">As permissões delegadas Files.Read.Selected e Files.ReadWrite.Selected são válidas apenas em contas corporativas ou de estudante e são expostas apenas para trabalhar com [manipuladores (v1.0) de arquivos do Office 365](https://msdn.microsoft.com/office/office365/howto/using-cross-suite-apps). Elas não devem ser usadas para chamar diretamente as APIs do Microsoft Graph.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p144">The Files.Read.Selected and Files.ReadWrite.Selected delegated permissions are only valid on work or school accounts and are only exposed for working with [Office 365 file handlers (v1.0)](https://msdn.microsoft.com/office/office365/howto/using-cross-suite-apps). They should not be used for directly calling Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1049">A permissão delegada Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder só é válida para contas pessoais e é usada para acessar a [pasta especial da Raiz de Aplicativo](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm) com a API do Microsoft Graph [Obter pasta especial](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder?view=graph-rest-1.0) do OneDrive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1049">The Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder delegated permission is only valid for personal accounts and is used for accessing the [App Root special folder](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm) with the OneDrive [Get special folder](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder?view=graph-rest-1.0) Microsoft Graph API.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1050">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1050">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1051">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1051">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1052">_Files.Read_: Ler arquivos armazenados no OneDrive do usuário conectado (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1052">_Files.Read_: Read files stored in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1053">_Files.Read.All_: Ler arquivos compartilhados com o usuário conectado (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1053">_Files.Read.All_: Read files shared with the signed-in user (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1054">_Files.ReadWrite_: Gravar um arquivo no OneDrive do usuário conectado (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1054">_Files.ReadWrite_: Write a file in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1055">_Files.ReadWrite.All_: Gravar um arquivo compartilhado com o usuário (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1055">_Files.ReadWrite.All_: Write a file shared with the user (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1056">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_: Gravar arquivos na pasta do aplicativo do OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1056">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_: Write files into the app's folder in OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1057">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1057">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1137">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1137">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1138">A funcionalidade de grupo não é compatível com contas pessoais da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1138">Group functionality is not supported on personal Microsoft accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1139">Para grupos do Office 365, as Permissões de grupo concedem ao aplicativo acesso ao conteúdo do grupo. Por exemplo, conversas, arquivos, anotações e assim por diante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1139">For Office 365 groups, Group permissions grant the app access to the contents of the group; for example, conversations, files, notes, and so on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p154">No caso de Permissões de aplicativo, há algumas limitações para APIs com suporte. Confira mais informações em [problemas conhecidos](known-issues.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p154">For application permissions, there are some limitations for the APIs that are supported. For more information, see [known issues](known-issues.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p155">Em alguns casos, um aplicativo pode precisar de [Permissões de diretório](#directory-permissions) para ler algumas propriedades do grupo como `member` e `memberOf`. Por exemplo, se um grupo tiver um ou mais [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta) como membros, o aplicativo precisará de permissões eficazes para ler as entidades de serviço através do recebimento de uma das _Permissões de diretório\*_, caso contrário, o Microsoft Graph retornará um erro. No caso de Permissões Delegadas, o usuário conectado deve ter privilégios suficientes na organização para ler as entidades de serviço. A mesma orientação se aplica à propriedade `memberOf` que pode retornar [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p155">In some cases, an app may need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions) to read some group properties like `member` and `memberOf`. For example, if a group has a one or more [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta) as members, the app will need effective permissions to read service principals through being granted one of the _Directory.\*_ permissions, otherwise Microsoft Graph will return an error. (In the case of delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to read service principals.) The same guidance applies for the `memberOf` property, which can return [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1145">Para definir o atributo **preferredDataLocation** de um grupo do Office 365, um aplicativo precisa da permissão Directory.ReadWrite.All.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1145">To set an Office 365 group's **preferredDataLocation** attribute, an app needs Directory.ReadWrite.All permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1146">Quando os usuários em um ambiente multigeográfico criam um grupo do Office 365, o valor**preferredDataLocation** para o grupo é definido automaticamente como sendo igual ao do usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1146">When users in a multi-geo environment create an Office 365 group, the **preferredDataLocation** value for the group is automatically set to that of the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1147">Para saber mais sobre o local de dados preferencial dos grupos, confira [Criar um grupo do Office 365 com uma PDL específica](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/multi-geo-add-group-with-pdl).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1147">For more information about groups' preferred data location, see [Create an Office 365 group with a specific PDL](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/multi-geo-add-group-with-pdl).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p157">As permissões de grupo são usadas para controlar o acesso aos recursos e APIs do [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview). Não há suporte para as contas pessoais da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p157">Group permissions are used to control access to [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview) resources and APIs. Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p158">As Permissões de grupo também são usadas para controlar o acesso a APIs e recursos do [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview). Somente as permissões delegadas são suportadas pelas APIs do Microsoft Planner; as permissões de aplicativo não são suportadas. Contas pessoais da Microsoft não são suportadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p158">Group permissions are also used to control access to [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview) resources and APIs. Only delegated permissions are supported for Microsoft Planner APIs; application permissions are not supported. Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1153">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1153">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1154">Delegated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1154">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1155">_Group.Read.All_: Ler todos os grupos do Office 365 dos quais o usuário conectado é membro (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1155">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Office 365 groups that the signed-in user is a member of (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1156">_Group.Read.All_: Ler todo o conteúdo do grupo do Office 365, como conversas (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1156">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Office 365 group content like conversations (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1157">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Atualizar propriedades do grupo, como fotografias (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1157">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Update group properties, like photo (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1158">_GroupMember.ReadWrite.All_: Atualizar os membros do grupo (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1158">_GroupMember.ReadWrite.All_: Update group members (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`).</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1159">**Observação:** Isso também requer o _User.ReadBasic.All_ para ler o usuário para adicionar como membro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1159">**Note:**: This also requires _User.ReadBasic.All_ to read the user to add as a member.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1160">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1160">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1161">_Group.Read.All_: Localizar todos os grupos com nomes que começam com "Vendas" (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1161">_Group.Read.All_: Find all groups with name that starts with 'Sales' (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1162">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: O serviço daemon cria novos eventos no calendário de um grupo do Office 365 (`POST /groups/{id}/events`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1162">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Daemon service creates new events on an Office 365 group's calendar (`POST /groups/{id}/events`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1163">_Group.Create_: Criar um novo grupo (`POST /groups`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1163">_Group.Create_: Creates a new group (`POST /groups`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1164">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1164">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

---

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1182">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1182">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1183">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_ e _IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ são válidos apenas para contas corporativas ou de estudantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1183">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_ and _IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1184">Para que um aplicativo leia ou grave provedores de identidade com permissões delegadas, o usuário conectado deve ter a função de Administrador Global.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1184">For an app to read or write identity providers with delegated permissions, the signed-in user must be assigned the Global Administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1185">Para obter mais informações sobre funções de administrador, confira [Atribuindo funções de administrador no Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1185">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1186">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1186">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1187">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1187">Delegated</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1188">Os seguintes usos são válidos para permissões delegadas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1188">The following usages are valid for both delegated permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1189">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Leia todos os provedores de identidade configurados no locatário (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1189">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read all identity providers configured in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1190">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Leia um provedor de identidade existente (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1190">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read an existing identity provider (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1191">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Crie um provedor de identidade (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1191">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Create an identity provider (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1192">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Atualize um provedor de identidade existente (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1192">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Update an existing identity provider (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1193">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Exclua um provedor de identidade existente (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1193">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Delete an existing identity provider (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1194">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1194">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

## <a name="identity-risk-event-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1195">Permissões de eventos de risco de identidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1195">Identity risk event permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1216">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1216">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p160">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ é válido apenas para contas corporativas ou de estudante. No caso de um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para ler as informações de risco de identidade, o usuário conectado deve ser um membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global, Administrador de Segurança ou funções do Leitor de Segurança. Para obter mais informações sobre funções de administrador, confira [Atribuindo funções de administrador no Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p160">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ is valid only for work or school accounts. For an app with delegated permissions to read identity risk information, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, or Security Reader. For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1220">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1220">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1221">Permissões delegadas e de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1221">Delegated and Application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1222">Os seguintes usos são válidos para Permissões Delegadas e Permissões de aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1222">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1223">Ler todos os eventos de risco gerados para todos os usuários do locatário (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1223">Read all risk events generated for all users in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1224">Ler todos os eventos de risco de malware gerados pelo botnet Dorknet (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1224">Read malware risk events generated by the Dorknet botnet (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1225">Ler os mais recentes 50 eventos de risco (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents?$orderBy=riskEventDateTime desc&top=50`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1225">Read most recent 50 risk events (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents?$orderBy=riskEventDateTime desc&top=50`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1226">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1226">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>
