### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1393">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1393">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1394">**Observação:** O uso das APIs do Microsoft Graph para configurar controles e políticas do Intune ainda exige que o serviço do Intune seja [corretamente licenciado](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) pelo cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1394">**Note:** Using the Microsoft Graph APIs to configure Intune controls and policies still requires that the Intune service is [correctly licensed](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) by the customer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1395">Essas permissões só são válidas para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1395">These permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1396">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1396">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1397">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1397">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1398">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_: Verificar o estado atual da assinatura do Intune (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1398">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_: Check the current state of the Intune subscription (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1399">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Criar novos Termos e Condições (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1399">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Create new Terms and Conditions (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1400">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_: Localizar o status da configuração de um dispositivo (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1400">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_: Find the status of a device configuration (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1401">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Atribuir uma política de conformidade do dispositivo para um grupo (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1401">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Assign a device compliance policy to a group (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`).</span></span>

Não inclui a permissão para enviar emails.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p171">Allows the app to read user's mailbox settings without a signed-in user. Does not include permission to send mail.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1507">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1507">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1508">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1508">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1509">Ler e gravar todas as configurações de caixa de correio do usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1509">Read and write all user mailbox settings</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p172">Permite que o aplicativo crie, leia, atualize e exclua as configurações da caixa de correio sem um usuário conectado. Não inclui a permissão para enviar emails.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p172">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete user's mailbox settings without a signed-in user. Does not include permission to send mail.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1512">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1512">Yes</span></span> |

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1513">Os Administradores **Importantes** podem configurar a [política de acesso ao aplicativo](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) para limitar o acesso do aplicativo às caixas de correio _específicas_ e não a todas as caixas de correio na organização, mesmo que as permissões de aplicativo do Mail.Read, Mail.ReadWrite, Mail.Send, MailboxSettings.Read, ou MailboxSettings.ReadWrite sejam concedidas ao aplicativo. </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1513">**Important** Administrators can configure [application access policy](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) to limit app access to _specific_ mailboxes and not to all the mailboxes in the organization, even if the app has been granted the application permissions of Mail.Read, Mail.ReadWrite, Mail.Send, MailboxSettings.Read, or MailboxSettings.ReadWrite.</span></span>


### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1514">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1514">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p173">_Mail.Read.Shared_, _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_, e _Mail.Send.Shared_ só são válidos para contas corporativas ou de estudante. Todas as demais permissões são válidas tanto para contas da Microsoft como para contas corporativas e de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p173">_Mail.Read.Shared_, _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_, and _Mail.Send.Shared_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1517">Com a permissão _Mail.Send_ ou _Mail.Send.Shared_, um aplicativo pode enviar emails e salvar uma cópia na pasta Itens Enviados do usuário, mesmo se o aplicativo não usar uma permissão _Mail.ReadWrite_ ou _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ correspondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1517">With the _Mail.Send_ or _Mail.Send.Shared_ permission, an app can send mail and save a copy to the user's Sent Items folder, even if the app does not use a corresponding _Mail.ReadWrite_ or _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ permission.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1518">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1518">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1519">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1519">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1520">_Mail.Read_: Listar mensagens na caixa de entrada do usuário classificadas por `receivedDateTime` (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1520">_Mail.Read_: List messages in the user's inbox, sorted by `receivedDateTime` (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1521">_Mail.Read.Shared_: Localizar todas as mensagens com anexos na caixa de entrada de um usuário que compartilhou sua caixa de entrada com o usuário conectado (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1521">_Mail.Read.Shared_: Find all messages with attachments in a user's inbox that has shared their inbox with the signed-in user (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1522">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Marcar uma mensagem lida (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1522">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Mark a message read (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1523">_Mail.Send_: Enviar uma mensagem (`POST /me/sendmail`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1523">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /me/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1524">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_: Atualizar a resposta automática do usuário (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1524">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_: Update the user's automatic reply (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1525">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1525">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1526">_Mail.Read_: Localizar mensagens de pedro@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1526">_Mail.Read_: Find messages from bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1527">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Criar uma nova pasta na Caixa de Entrada chamada `Expense Reports` (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1527">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Create a new folder in the Inbox named `Expense Reports` (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1528">_Mail.Send_: Enviar uma mensagem (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1528">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1529">_MailboxSettings.Read_: Obter o fuso horário padrão para a caixa de correio do usuário (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1529">_MailboxSettings.Read_: Get the default timezone for the user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1530">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1530">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1552">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1552">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1553">_Member.Read.Hidden_ é válida somente para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1553">_Member.Read.Hidden_ is valid only on work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p174">A associação pode estar oculta em alguns grupos do Office 365. Isso significa que somente os membros do grupo podem exibir seus membros. Esse recurso pode ser usado para ajudar a cumprir regulamentos que exijam a ocultação da associação do grupo de pessoas externas (por exemplo, um grupo do Office 365 que representa os alunos registrados em uma classe).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p174">Membership in some Office 365 groups can be hidden. This means that only the members of the group can view its members. This feature can be used to help comply with regulations that require an organization to hide group membership from outsiders (for example, an Office 365 group that represents students enrolled in a class).</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1597">_Notes.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1597">_Notes.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1598">Acesso limitado ao bloco de anotações (preterido)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1598">Limited notebook access (deprecated)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1599">**Preterido**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1599">**Deprecated**</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="453f9-p175">Não usar. ### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1617">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1617">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p176">_Notes.Read.All_ e _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ só são válidos para contas corporativas ou de estudante. Todas as demais permissões são válidas tanto para contas da Microsoft como para contas corporativas e de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p176">_Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1620">Com a permissão _Notes.Create_, um aplicativo pode exibir a hierarquia do bloco de anotações do OneNote do usuário conectado e criar conteúdo do OneNote (blocos de anotações, grupos de seção, seções, páginas, etc.).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1620">With the _Notes.Create_ permission, an app can view the OneNote notebook hierarchy of the signed-in user and create OneNote content (notebooks, section groups, sections, pages, etc.).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1621">_Notes.ReadWrite_ e _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ também permitem que o aplicativo modifique as permissões no conteúdo do OneNote que pode ser acessado pelo usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1621">_Notes.ReadWrite_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ also allow the app to modify the permissions on the OneNote content that can be accessed by the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1622">Para contas corporativas ou de estudante, _Notes.Read.All_ e _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ permitem que o aplicativo acesse o conteúdo do OneNote de outros usuários ao qual o usuário conectado tenha permissão dentro da organização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1622">For work or school accounts, _Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ allow the app to access other users' OneNote content that the signed-in user has permission to within the organization.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1623">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1623">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1624">Delegated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1624">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1625">_Notes.Create_: Criar novos blocos de anotações para o usuário conectado (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1625">_Notes.Create_: Create a new notebooks for the signed-in user (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1626">_Notes.Read_: Criar blocos de anotações para o usuário conectado (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1626">_Notes.Read_: Read the notebooks for the signed-in user (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1627">_Notes.Read.All_: Obter todos os blocos de anotações aos quais o usuário conectado tenha acesso dentro da organização (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1627">_Notes.Read.All_: Get all notebooks that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1628">_Notes.ReadWrite_: Atualizar a página do usuário conectado (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1628">_Notes.ReadWrite_: Update the page of the signed-in user (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1629">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Criar uma página no bloco de anotações de outro usuário ao qual o usuário conectado tenha acesso dentro da organização (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1629">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Create a page in another user's notebook that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1630">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1630">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1631">_Notes.Read.All_: Ler todos os blocos de anotações de usuários em um grupo (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1631">_Notes.Read.All_: Read all users notebooks in a group (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1632">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Atualizar a página em um bloco de anotações para qualquer usuário da organização (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1632">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Update the page in a notebook for any user in the organization (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1633">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1633">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1647">A restrição *CreatedByApp* associada a essa permissão indica que o serviço aplicará filtragem implícita aos resultados com base na identidade aplicativo que realizar a chamada, seja a ID de aplicativo da conta  Microsoft ou um conjunto de IDs de aplicativos configurados para uma identidade de aplicativo de plataformas cruzadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1647">The *CreatedByApp* constraint associated with this permission indicates that the service will apply implicit filtering to results based on the identity of the calling app, either the Microsoft account app ID or a set of app IDs configured for a cross-platform application identity.</span></span>

Publique uma notificação centrada no usuário, que pode ser entregue aos vários clientes do aplicativo em execução em pontos de extremidade diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1650">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish a user-centric notification, which might then be delivered to the user’s multiple application clients running on different endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1651">(POSTAGEM/me/notificações /).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1651">(POST /me/notifications/).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1742">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1742">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p180">Você pode usar essas permissões para especificar os artefatos que deseja que sejam retornados nas solicitações de token e de autorização do Azure AD. O suporte a elas é oferecido de formas diferentes nos pontos de extremidade v 1.0 e v 2.0. do Azure AD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p180">You can use these permissions to specify artifacts that you want returned in Azure AD authorization and token requests. They are supported differently by the Azure AD v1.0 and v2.0 endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p181">Com o ponto de extremidade (v 1.0) do Azure AD, somente a permissão _openid_ é usada. Você especifica no parâmetro *scope*, na solicitação de autorização, para retornar um token de ID quando usar o protocolo OpenID Connect para conectar um usuário ao seu aplicativo. Para saber mais, confira o artigo [Autorizar o acesso aos aplicativos web usando o OpenID Connect e o Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code). Para retornar com êxito um token de ID, você também deve garantir que a permissão _User.Read_ esteja configurada quando você registrar seu aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p181">With the Azure AD (v1.0) endpoint, only the _openid_ permission is used. You specify it in the *scope* parameter in an authorization request to return an ID token when you use the OpenID Connect protocol to sign in a user to your app. For more information, see [Authorize access to web applications using OpenID Connect and Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code). To successfully return an ID token, you must also make sure that the _User.Read_ permission is configured when you register your app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p182">Com o ponto de extremidade v 2.0 do Azure AD, você especifica a permissão _offline\_access_ no parâmetro _scope_ para solicitar explicitamente um token de atualização quando estiver usando os protocolos OAuth 2.0 ou OpenID Connect. Com o OpenID Connect, você especifica a permissão _openid_ para solicitar um token de ID. Também é possível especificar a permissão _email_, a permissão _profile_, ou ambas, para retornar declarações adicionais no token de ID. Você não precisa especificar a _User.Read_ para retornar um token de ID com o ponto de extremidade v 2.0. Para saber mais, confira os [escopos do OpenID Connect](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p182">With the Azure AD v2.0 endpoint, you specify the _offline\_access_ permission in the _scope_ parameter to explicitly request a refresh token when using the OAuth 2.0 or OpenID Connect protocols. With OpenID Connect, you specify the _openid_ permission to request an ID token. You can also specify the _email_ permission, _profile_ permission, or both to return additional claims in the ID token. You do not need to specify _User.Read_ to return an ID token with the v2.0 endpoint. For more information, see [OpenID Connect scopes](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p183">**Importante** A Biblioteca de Autenticação da Microsoft (MSAL) atualmente especifica as permissões _offline\_access_, _openid_, _profile_ e _email_ por padrão nas solicitações de autorização e de token. Isso significa que, para o caso padrão, se você especificar explicitamente essas permissões, o Azure AD pode retornar um erro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p183">**Important** The Microsoft Authentication Library (MSAL) currently specifies _offline\_access_, _openid_, _profile_, and _email_ by default in authorization and token requests. This means that, for the default case, if you specify these permissions explicitly, Azure AD may return an error.</span></span>

---

## <a name="organizational-contact-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1796">Permissões de contato organizacional</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1796">Organizational contact permissions</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-1941">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1941">Example usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-1942">Os seguintes usos são válidos para permissões delegadas e permissões de aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1942">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1945">_Policy.Read.All_: Ler as políticas de distribuição de recursos da sua organização (`GET /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1945">_Policy.Read.All_: Read your organization's feature rollout policies (`GET /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1946">_Policy.ReadWrite.ApplicationConfiguration: leia e grave as políticas de configuração dos aplicativos da sua organização (`POST /beta/policies/tokenLifetimePolicies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1946">_Policy.ReadWrite.ApplicationConfiguration: Read and write your organization's application configuration policies (`POST /beta/policies/tokenLifetimePolicies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1947">_Policy.ReadWrite.ConditionalAccess_: Leia e escreva as políticas de acesso condicional da sua organização (`POST /beta/identity/conditionalAccess/policies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1947">_Policy.ReadWrite.ConditionalAccess_: Read and write your organization's conditional access policies (`POST /beta/identity/conditionalAccess/policies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-1948">_Policy.ReadWrite.FeatureRollout_: Ler e gravar todas as políticas de distribuição de recursos da sua organização (`POST /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-1948">_Policy.ReadWrite.FeatureRollout_: Read and write your organization's feature rollout policies (`POST /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2001">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2001">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2002">_ProgramControl.Read.All_ e _ProgramControl.ReadWrite.All_ são válidos apenas para contas de trabalho ou escola.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2002">_ProgramControl.Read.All_ and _ProgramControl.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2003">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para ler programas e controles de programas, o usuário conectado deve ser membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global, Administrador de Segurança, Leitor de Segurança ou Administrador de Usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2003">For an app with delegated permissions to read programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2004">Para um aplicativo com permissões delegadas para gravar programas e controles de programas, o usuário conectado deve ser membro de uma das seguintes funções de administrador: Administrador Global ou Administrador do Usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2004">For an app with delegated permissions to write programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2005">Para obter mais informações sobre funções de administrador, confira [Atribuindo funções de administrador no Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2005">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2029">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2029">Remarks</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2030">As permissões de relatórios só são válidas para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2030">Reports permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2031">Para as permissões delegadas permitirem que aplicativos leiam relatórios de uso de serviço em nome de um usuário, o administrador de locatários deve atribuir ao usuário uma função de administrador limitada do Azure AD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2031">For delegated permissions to allow apps to read service usage reports on behalf of a user, the tenant administrator must have assigned the user an Azure AD limited administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2032">Para saber mais, confira [Autorização para APIs lerem os relatórios de uso do Office 365](reportroot-authorization.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2032">For more details, see [Authorization for APIs to read Office 365 usage reports](reportroot-authorization.md).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2073">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2073">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2074">Com a permissão _RoleManagement.Read.Directory_ um aplicativo pode ler directoryRoles e directoryRoleTemplates.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2074">With the _RoleManagement.Read.Directory_ permission an application can read directoryRoles and directoryRoleTemplates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2075">Isso inclui a leitura de informações de associação para funções de diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2075">This includes reading membership information for directory roles.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2076">Com a permissão _RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_, um aplicativo pode ler e gravar directoryRoles (directoryRoleTemplates são recursos somente leitura).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2076">With the _RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_ permission an application can read and write directoryRoles (directoryRoleTemplates are readonly resources).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2077">Isso inclui adicionar e remover membros de funções de diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2077">This includes adding and removing members to and from directory roles.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2078">As permissões de relatórios só são válidas para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2078">Role management permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2079">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2079">Example usage</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2080">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Ler a lista de modelos de função disponíveis(`GET /directoryRoleTemplates`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2080">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of available role templates (`GET /directoryRoleTemplates`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2081">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Ler a lista de funções ativadas em seu diretório(`GET /directoryRoles`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2081">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of activated roles in your directory (`GET /directoryRoles`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2082">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Ler a lista de membros para uma função (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2082">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of members for a role (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2083">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Ler a lista de membros com escopo de unidade administrativa para uma função (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2083">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of administrative unit-scoped members for a role (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2084">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Ativar uma função de diretório a partir de um modelo de função (`POST /directoryRoles`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2084">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Activate a directory role from a role template  (`POST /directoryRoles`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2085">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Adicionar um membro a uma função de diretório (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2085">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Add a member to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2086">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Adicionar um membro de escopo de unidade administrativa a uma função de diretório(`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2086">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Add an administrative unit-scoped member to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2087">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2087">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2128">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2128">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2129">As permissões de pesquisa só são válidas para contas corporativas ou de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2129">Search permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2130">Esta permissão de pesquisa só se aplica aos dados ingeridos da API de indexação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2130">This search permission is only applicable to ingested data from the indexing API.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2131">O acesso aos dados por meio de pesquisa requer a devida permissão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2131">Access to data via search requires the corresponding permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2132">Por exemplo, _Files.Read.All_ para acessar arquivos por meio da pesquisa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2132">Ex : _Files.Read.All_ to access files via search.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2134">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2134">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2135">_ExternalItem.Read.All__: acessar dados externos da [API de pesquisa](/graph/api/resources/search-api-overview) (`POST /search/query`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2135">_ExternalItem.Read.All__:  Access external data from the [search API](/graph/api/resources/search-api-overview) (`POST /search/query`).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2207">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2207">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2208">Permissões delegadas e de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2208">Delegated and Application</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2209">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_: Ler a lista de todos os alertas de segurança de todos os provedores de segurança licenciados disponíveis para o seu locatário (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2209">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_: Read the list of all security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2210">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_: Atualize ou leia os alertas de segurança de todos os provedores de segurança licenciados disponíveis para o seu locatário (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2210">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_: Update or read security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant  (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2261">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2261">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2262">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2262">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2266">_Sites.FullControl.All_: Acesso completo a sites e listas do SharePoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2266">_Sites.FullControl.All_: Complete access to SharePoint sites and lists.</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2294">Permissões de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2294">Application permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2295">Nenhum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2295">None.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2296">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2296">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p211">As permissões de _tarefas_ são usadas para controlar o acesso de tarefas do Outlook. O acesso a tarefas do Microsoft Planner é controlado pelas permissões do [_Grupo_](#group-permissions).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p211">_Tasks_ permissions are used to control access for Outlook tasks. Access for Microsoft Planner tasks is controlled by [_Group_ permissions](#group-permissions).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p212">As permissões _Compartilhadas_ atualmente só são compatíveis com contas corporativas ou de estudante. Mesmo com permissões _Compartilhadas_, as leituras e gravações podem falhar se o usuário que possui o conteúdo compartilhado não tiver concedido as permissões de usuário de acesso para modificar o conteúdo dentro da pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p212">_Shared_ permissions are currently only supported for work or school accounts. Even with _Shared_ permissions, reads and writes may fail if the user who owns the shared content has not granted the accessing user permissions to modify content within the folder.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2301">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2301">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2302">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2302">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2303">_Tasks.Read_: Obter todas as tarefas na caixa de correio do usuário (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2303">_Tasks.Read_: Get all tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2304">_Tasks.Read.Shared_: Acessar tarefas em uma pasta compartilhada com você por outro usuário em sua organização (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2304">_Tasks.Read.Shared_: Access tasks in a folder shared to you by another user in your organization (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2305">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Adicionar um evento à pasta de tarefas padrão do usuário (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2305">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's default task folder (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2306">_Tasks.Read_: Obter todas as tarefas não concluídas na caixa de correio do usuário (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2306">_Tasks.Read_: Get all uncompleted tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2307">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Atualizar uma tarefa na caixa de correio do usuário (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2307">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Update a task in a user's mailbox (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2308">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_: Concluir uma tarefa em nome de outro usuário (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2308">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_: Complete a task on behalf of another user (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2309">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2309">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

## <a name="user-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2659">Permissões do usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2659">User permissions</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2666">_User.Read_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2666">_User.Read_</span></span>       |    <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2667">Entrar e ler o perfil do usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2667">Sign-in and read user profile</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p227">Permite aos usuários entrar no aplicativo e permite ao aplicativo ler o perfil de usuários conectados. Também permite que o aplicativo leia as informações básicas da empresa sobre os usuários conectados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p227">Allows users to sign-in to the app, and allows the app to read the profile of signed-in users. | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2672">_User.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2672">_User.ReadWrite_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2673">Acesso de leitura e gravação ao perfil de usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2673">Read and write access to user profile</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2674">Permite que o aplicativo leia o perfil completo do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2674">Allows the app to read the signed-in user's full profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2675">Também possibilita que o aplicativo atualize as informações de perfil do usuário conectado em seu nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2675">It also allows the app to update the signed-in user's profile information on their behalf.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2676">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2676">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2677">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2677">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2678">_User.ReadBasic.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2678">_User.ReadBasic.All_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2679">Ler os perfis básicos de todos usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2679">Read all users' basic profiles</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2680">Permite ao aplicativo ler um conjunto básico de propriedades de perfil de outros usuários em sua organização em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2680">Allows the app to read a basic set of profile properties of other users in your organization on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2681">Inclui o nome para exibição, nome e sobrenome, endereço de email, extensões abertas e foto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2681">This includes display name, first and last name, email address, open extensions and photo.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2682">Também permite que o aplicativo leia o perfil completo do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2682">Also allows the app to read the full profile of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2683">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2683">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2684">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2684">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2685">_User.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2685">_User.Read.All_</span></span>  |     <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2686">Ler os perfis completos de todos os usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2686">Read all users' full profiles</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2687">Permite ao aplicativo ler o conjunto completo de propriedades do perfil, relatórios e gerentes de outros usuários em sua organização, em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2687">Allows the app to read the full set of profile properties, reports, and managers of other users in your organization, on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2688">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2688">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2689">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2689">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2690">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2690">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |     <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2691">Ler e gravar os perfis completos de todos os usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2691">Read and write all users' full profiles</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p230">Permite ao aplicativo ler e gravar o conjunto completo de propriedades do perfil, relatórios e gerentes de outros usuários na sua organização, em nome do usuário conectado. Também permite que o aplicativo crie e exclua usuários, além de redefinir senhas de usuário em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p230">Allows the app to read and write the full set of profile properties, reports, and managers of other users in your organization, on behalf of the signed-in user. Also allows the app to create and delete users as well as reset user passwords on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2694">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2694">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2695">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2695">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2696">_User.Invite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2696">_User.Invite.All_</span></span>  |     <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2697">Convidar usuários convidados para a organização</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2697">Invite guest users to the organization</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2698">Permite que o aplicativo convide usuários para sua organização em nome do usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2698">Allows the app to invite guest users to your organization, on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2699">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2699">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2700">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2700">No</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2706">_User.ManageIdentities.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2706">_User.ManageIdentities.All_</span></span>       |    <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2707">Gerenciar identidades de usuário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2707">Manage user identities</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2708">Permite que um aplicativo leia, atualize e exclua identidades associadas a uma conta de usuário à qual o usuário conectado tenha acesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2708">Allows an application to read, update and delete identities that are associated with a user's account, that the signed-in user has access to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2709">Controla quais identidades os seus usuários podem usar para entrar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2709">This controls which identities your users can sign-in with.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2710">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2710">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2711">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2711">No</span></span> |


#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2712">Permissões de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2712">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2713">Permissão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2713">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2714">Exibir Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2714">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2715">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2715">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2716">Consentimento Obrigatório do Administrador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2716">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2721">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2721">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2722">Ler e gravar os perfis completos de todos os usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2722">Read and write all users' full profiles</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-p232">Permite ao aplicativo ler e gravar o conjunto completo de propriedades do perfil, relatórios e gerentes de outros usuários na sua organização, sem um usuário conectado.  Também permite que o aplicativo crie e exclua usuários não administrativos. Não permite a redefinição de senhas de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p232">Allows the app to read and write the full set of profile properties, group membership, reports and managers of other users in your organization, without a signed-in user.  Also allows the app to create and delete non-administrative users. Does not allow reset of user passwords.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2726">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2726">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2727">_User.Invite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2727">_User.Invite.All_</span></span>  |     <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2728">Convidar usuários convidados para a organização</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2728">Invite guest users to the organization</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2729">Permite que o aplicativo convide usuários para sua organização sem um usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2729">Allows the app to invite guest users to your organization, without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2730">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2730">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2740">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2740">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p234">Com a permissão _User.Read_, um aplicativo também pode ler as informações básicas da empresa do usuário conectado de uma conta corporativa ou de estudante através do recurso [Organização](/graph/api/resources/organization?view=graph-rest-1.0). As propriedades a seguir estão disponíveis: id, displayName e verifiedDomains.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p234">With the _User.Read_ permission, an app can also read the basic company information of the signed-in user for a work or school account through the [organization](/graph/api/resources/organization?view=graph-rest-1.0) resource. The following properties are available: id, displayName, and verifiedDomains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p235">Para contas corporativas ou de estudante, o perfil completo inclui todas as propriedades declaradas do recurso [Usuário](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0). No caso das leituras, somente um número limitado de propriedades é retornado por padrão. Para ler propriedades que não estão no conjunto padrão, use `$select`. As propriedades padrão são:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p235">For work or school accounts, the full profile includes all of the declared properties of the [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) resource. On reads, only a limited number of properties are returned by default. To read properties that are not in the default set, use `$select`. The default properties are:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2747">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2747">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2748">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2748">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2749">jobTitle</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2749">jobTitle</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2750">Email</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2750">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2751">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2751">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2752">officeLocation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2752">officeLocation</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2753">preferredLanguage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2753">preferredLanguage</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2754">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2754">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2755">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2755">userPrincipalName</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2756">As Permissões Delegadas _User.ReadWrite_ e _User.Readwrite.All_ permitem ao aplicativo atualizar as seguintes propriedades de perfil de contas corporativas ou de estudante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2756">_User.ReadWrite_ and _User.Readwrite.All_ delegated permissions allow the app to update the following profile properties for work or school accounts:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2757">aboutMe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2757">aboutMe</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2758">birthday</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2758">birthday</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2759">hireDate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2759">hireDate</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2760">interests</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2760">interests</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2761">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2761">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2762">mySite</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2762">mySite</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2763">pastProjects</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2763">pastProjects</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2764">photo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2764">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2765">preferredName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2765">preferredName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2766">responsibilities</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2766">responsibilities</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2767">schools</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2767">schools</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2768">skills</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2768">skills</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2769">Com a Permissão de aplicativo _User.ReadWrite.All_, o aplicativo pode atualizar todas as propriedades declaradas das contas corporativas ou de estudante, com exceção da senha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2769">With the _User.ReadWrite.All_ application permission, the app can update all of the declared properties of work or school accounts except for password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2770">Com a permissão _User.ReadWrite.All_ delegada ou de aplicativo, a atualização de **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone** ou **otherMails** de outro usuário é permitida apenas em usuários que não são administradores ou que tenham uma das seguintes funções: Leitor de Diretório, Emissor de Convites Independente, Leitor do Centro de Mensagens e Leitor de Relatórios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2770">With the _User.ReadWrite.All_ delegated or application permission, updating another user's **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone** or **otherMails** is only allowed on users who are non-administrators or assigned one of the following roles: Directory Readers, Guest Inviter, Message Center Reader and Reports Reader.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2771">Para obter mais detalhes, confira Administrador de suporte técnico (senha) nas [funções disponíveis do Azure AD](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2771">For more details, see Helpdesk (Password) Administrator in [Azure AD available roles](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2772">Para ler ou gravar os subordinados diretos (`directReports`) ou o gerente (`manager`) de uma conta corporativa ou de estudante, o aplicativo deve ter as permissões _User.Read.All_ (somente leitura) ou _User.ReadWrite.All_.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2772">To read or write direct reports (`directReports`) or the manager (`manager`) of a work or school account, the app must have either _User.Read.All_ (read only) or _User.ReadWrite.All_.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p237">A permissão _User.ReadBasic.All_ restringe o acesso do aplicativo a um conjunto limitado de propriedades conhecido como o perfil básico. Isso ocorre porque o perfil completo pode conter informações de diretório confidenciais. O perfil básico inclui apenas as seguintes propriedades:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p237">The _User.ReadBasic.All_ permission constrains app access to a limited set of properties known as the basic profile. This is because the full profile might contain sensitive directory information. The basic profile includes only the following properties:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2776">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2776">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2777">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2777">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2778">Email</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2778">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2779">Foto</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2779">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2780">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2780">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2781">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2781">userPrincipalName</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p238">Para ler as associações de grupos de um usuário (`memberOf`), o aplicativo deve ter o [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) ou o [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions). No entanto, se o usuário também tiver uma associação a um [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole?view=graph-rest-1.0) ou [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta), o aplicativo também precisará de permissões efetivas para ler esses recursos ou o Microsoft Graph retornará um erro. Isso significa que o aplicativo deve ter também [Permissões do diretório](#directory-permissions); para as Permissões Delegadas, o usuário conectado deve ter privilégios suficientes na organização para acessar unidades administrativas e funções de diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p238">To read the group memberships of a user (`memberOf`), the app must have either [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) or [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions). However, if the user also has membership in a [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole?view=graph-rest-1.0) or an [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta), the app will need effective permissions to read those resources too, or Microsoft Graph will return an error. This means the app will also need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions), and, for delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to access directory roles and administrative units.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2785">Com o _User.ManageIdentities.All_ delegado ou as permissões de aplicativo, é possível atualizar as identidades (`identities`) de um usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2785">With the _User.ManageIdentities.All_ delegated or application permission, it is possible to update the identities (`identities`) of a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2786">Isso inclui as identidades federadas (ou identidades sociais) ou as identidades locais com nomes de entrada com base em nome ou email.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2786">This includes federated (or social identities) or local identities with email or name-based sign-in names.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2787">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2787">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2788">Delegated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2788">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2789">_User.Read_: Ler o perfil completo para o usuário conectado (`GET /me`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2789">_User.Read_: Read the full profile for the signed-in user (`GET /me`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2790">_User.ReadWrite_: Atualizar a foto do usuário conectado (`PUT /me/photo/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2790">_User.ReadWrite_: Update the photo of the signed-in user (`PUT /me/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2791">_User.ReadBasic.All_: Localizar todos os usuários cujos nomes começam com "Davi" (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2791">_User.ReadBasic.All_: Find all users whose name starts with "David" (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2792">_User.Read.All_: Ler o gerente de um usuário (`GET /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2792">_User.Read.All_: Read a user's manager (`GET /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2793">Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2793">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2794">_User.Read.All_: Ler todos os usuários e relações usando a consulta delta (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2794">_User.Read.All_: Read all users and relationships through delta query (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2795">_User.ReadWrite.All_: Atualizar a foto de qualquer usuário na organização (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2795">_User.ReadWrite.All_: Update the photo for any user in the organization (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2796">Para cenários mais complexos que envolvem várias permissões, confira [Cenários de permissões](#permission-scenarios).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2796">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2809">Permissões de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2809">Application permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2811">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2811">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2812">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* é válida tanto para contas da Microsoft como para contas corporativas e de estudante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2812">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* is valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2813">A restrição *CreatedByApp* associada a essa permissão indica que o serviço aplicará filtragem implícita aos resultados com base na identidade aplicativo que realizar a chamada, seja a ID de aplicativo MSA ou um conjunto de IDs de aplicativos configurados para uma identidade de aplicativo de plataformas cruzadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2813">The *CreatedByApp* constraint associated with this permission indicates the service will apply implicit filtering to results based on the identity of the calling app, either the MSA app id or a set of app ids configured for a cross-platform application identity.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2814">Exemplo de uso</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2814">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2815">Delegado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2815">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2816">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: obter uma lista de atividades de usuários recentes únicos com base nos itens de histórico associados publicados no último dia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2816">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Get a list of recent unique user activities based on associated history items published in the last day.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2817">(GET /me/activities/recent).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2817">(GET /me/activities/recent).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2818">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: publicar ou atualizar uma atividade do usuário que poderá ser retomada pelo usuário do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2818">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a user activity which may be resumed by the user of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2819">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2819">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2820">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: publicar ou atualizar um item de histórico de uma atividade de usuário especificada para representar o período de engajamento do usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2820">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a history item for a specified user activity in order to represent the period of user engagement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2821">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2821">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2822">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: excluir uma atividade de usuário em resposta a uma solicitação iniciada pelo usuário ou para remover dados inválidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2822">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a user activity in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2823">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2823">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2824">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: excluir um item de histórico em resposta a uma solicitação iniciada pelo usuário ou para remover dados inválidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2824">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a history item in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2825">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2825">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2859">Permissões de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2859">Application permissions</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2860">Permissão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2860">Permission</span></span>                              |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2861">Exibir Cadeia de Caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2861">Display String</span></span>                        |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2862">Descrição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2862">Description</span></span>        |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2863">Consentimento Obrigatório do Administrador</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2863">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:---------------------------------------|:-------------------------------------|:------------------|:----------------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2864">_UserAuthenticationMethod.Read.All_ (visualização privada)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2864">_UserAuthenticationMethod.Read.All_ (private preview)</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2865">Ler os métodos de autenticação dos usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2865">Read users' authentication methods</span></span>    |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2866">Permite que o aplicativo leia os métodos de autenticação de todos os usuários em sua organização sem um usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2866">Allows the app to read authentication methods of all users in your organization, without a signed-in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2867">Os métodos de autenticação incluem coisas como o número de telefone do usuário e as configurações do aplicativo Authenticator.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2867">Authentication methods include things like a user’s phone numbers and Authenticator app settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2868">Isso não permite que o aplicativo veja informações secretas, como senhas, entrar ou usar métodos de autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2868">This does not allow the app to see secret information like passwords, or to sign-in or otherwise use the authentication methods.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2869">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2869">Yes</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2870">_UserAuthenticationMethod.ReadWrite.All_ (visualização privada)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2870">_UserAuthenticationMethod.ReadWrite.All_ (private preview)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2871">Gerenciar os métodos de autenticação dos usuários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2871">Manage users' authentication methods</span></span>  |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2872">Permite que o aplicativo leia e grave os métodos de autenticação de todos os usuários em sua organização sem um usuário conectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2872">Allows the application to read and write authentication methods of all users in your organization, without a signed-in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2873">Os métodos de autenticação incluem coisas como o número de telefone do usuário e as configurações do aplicativo Authenticator.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2873">Authentication methods include things like a user’s phone numbers and Authenticator app settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2874">Isso não permite que o aplicativo veja informações secretas, como senhas, entrar ou usar métodos de autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2874">This does not allow the app to see secret information like passwords, or to sign-in or otherwise use the authentication methods.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2875">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2875">Yes</span></span>|

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2876">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2876">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2877">As permissões do método de autenticação do usuário são usadas para gerenciar os métodos de autenticação nos usuários.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2877">User authentication method permissions are used to manage authentication methods on users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2878">Com essas permissões, um usuário ou aplicativo delegado pode registrar novos métodos de autenticação em um usuário, ler os métodos de autenticação que o usuário já registrou, atualizar esses métodos de autenticação e removê-los do usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2878">With these permissions, a delegated user or application can register new authentication methods on a user, read the authentication methods the user already has registered, update those authentication methods, and remove them from the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-2879">Com essas permissões, todos os métodos de autenticação podem ser lidos e gerenciados em um usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2879">With these permissions, all authentication methods can be read and managed on a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2880">Isso inclui os métodos usados para:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2880">This includes methods used for:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2881">Autenticação primária (senha)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2881">Primary authentication (password)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2882">Segundo fator de autenticação multifator/MFA (números de telefone)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2882">Second factor of multi-factor authentication/MFA (phone numbers)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="453f9-2883">Redefinição de senha de autoatendimento/SSPR (endereço de email)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2883">Self-Service Password Reset/SSPR (email address)</span></span>

## <a name="permission-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="453f9-2884">Cenários de permissão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-2884">Permission scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="453f9-p253">Esta seção mostra alguns cenários comuns direcionados aos recursos [usuário](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) e [grupo](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) em uma organização. As tabelas mostram as permissões que um aplicativo precisa para conseguir executar operações específicas necessárias para o cenário. Observe que, em alguns casos, a capacidade do aplicativo de executar operações específicas dependerá se uma permissão é uma Permissão de aplicativo ou Permissão Delegada. No caso de Permissões Delegadas, as Permissões Efetivas do aplicativo também dependerão dos privilégios do usuário conectado na organização. Para obter mais informações, confira [Permissões delegadas, Permissões de aplicativo e permissões efetivas](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="453f9-p253">This section shows some common scenarios that target [user](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) and [group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) resources in an organization. The tables show the permissions that an app needs to be able to perform specific operations required by the scenario. Note that in some cases the ability of the app to perform specific operations will depend on whether a permission is an application or delegated permission. In the case of delegated permissions, the app's effective permissions will also depend on the privileges of the signed-in user within the organization. For more information, see  [Delegated permissions, Application permissions, and effective permissions](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions).</span></span>
